	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusSQLException.class.php') != 'bf44fca9fdd4d7086aaaf68b0a08e0e36557260d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusSQLException.class.php');

	}

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusSQLException.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/http_class.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php') != 'f5d22c1d86fc4081fd7eb6c2d5b3f644163b6ca9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/http_class.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/http_class.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/http_class.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php') !== 'f5d22c1d86fc4081fd7eb6c2d5b3f644163b6ca9') {

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/http_class.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/http_class.class.php') !== 'f5d22c1d86fc4081fd7eb6c2d5b3f644163b6ca9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/http_class.class.php');

if (!is_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') != 'd01415a1eadde32e60940c9d75287f72e3d6b821') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'd01415a1eadde32e60940c9d75287f72e3d6b821') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== '499490a9c2dbf47a46c8f6bdfa719f11342928d0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'd01415a1eadde32e60940c9d75287f72e3d6b821') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
		}
	}
}
